Built C: new pure `_pack_load_readiness(plh, race_pack_weight_kg)` → experience-led tier (**`established`** = `longest_carry ≥6 h` AND weight-covered [`heaviest ≥0.9×race_pack_weight`]; **`developing`** = `longest ≥2 h` OR `sessions ≥6`; **`limited`** otherwise) — a prior long carry outranks recent frequency. The `:615` render now emits the tier (`- pack_load_readiness: {tier} (heaviest_kg=…, longest_carry_hrs=…, recent_sessions_4wk=…, records=…)`, was the un-weighted `- pack_load_training: …`) + a Rule #15 `print` of the inputs + chosen tier. **Thresholds (`6.0`/`2.0`/`6`/`0.9`) are the one hand-tuned surface — flagged for Andy to retune.** **Part 2 (UX):** `templates/profile/edit.html` §C collapses the entry form behind a `<details class="pf-pack-add">` disclosure once any record exists (summary view; mirrors `event_windows.html`, CSP-clean); first-time entry shows the form directly; per-row Remove (delete) unchanged. **VERIFIED:** full suite **4022 passed / 30 skipped** (baseline 4015 + 7 new tests: `TestPackLoadReadiness` ×6 + the form-collapse render test; only the 3 pre-existing #217 warnings); ruff introduced **0** new errors (the 2 `layer3b/builder.py` `GoalViability`/`PeriodizationShape` unused imports pre-exist; `routes/profile.py` not touched). **2 substantive code files** (`layer3b/builder.py`, `templates/profile/edit.html`) + 2 test files — under ceiling. **No `layer0-apply` owed** — no schema change; the Layer-3B prompt text change re-keys the 3B cache → cold-recomputes once for pack-carrying athletes next deploy/regen (suppress-on-empty → no-pack athletes byte-identical; Andy is the only athlete). **#1067 closeable on merge.** **NEXT — Phase 1 continues:** #223 (pregnancy capture; HITL half deferred + re-confirm — `icebox`/`priority:low`), Phase 2 #394, Phase 3 #272/#267, then close epic #246. **STAY ON THE SIGN-UP/ONBOARDING THREAD. Before-start clamps to first block, past-end to last (Taper). **`derive_heat_acclim_state`** (§5.2) bands `HeatAcclimState` from `COUNT(DISTINCT date)` of hot training days (`temp_f > 77.0` = 25 °C) in `conditions_log` over 30 days (low 0–4 / moderate 5–13 / high ≥14), returning a `(state, data_sparse)` tuple — `data_sparse` (<5 logged condition-days) the consumer renders as `heat_acclim_data_sparse`; sparse forces `level='low'`. Derived at read time, **no new schema**. **`HeatAcclimState`** pydantic model added to `layer4/context.py` (spec §3 shape, locked to 2E's signature). `_INTERNAL_REGISTRY_KEYS` stripped from the overlay. **`app.py`** exempts the new cron from the session wall; **`vercel.json`** schedules it (`0 15 * * *`). **`tests/test_nudges_staleness.py`** (registry wiring, preference gating incl. fail-open + no-leak, reconcile-spec shape, cron route 401/auth + delete-then-insert counts). **VERIFIED:** full suite **3728 passed / 30 skipped** (only the 3 #217 warnings); ### Predecessor — #889 event windows (per-day volume levels)

**#889 EVENT WINDOWS — PER-DAY VOLUME LEVELS (per-DATE schedule within one reduced_volume window) (2026-06-29; branch `claude/issue-889-7ja7tu`; PR [#989](https://github.com/ahorn885/exercise/pull/989); issue [#889](https://github.com/ahorn885/exercise/issues/889) — go-live blocker, Andy-directed detour off the #884 thread).** A `reduced_volume` window scaled **every** covered day by its single `volume_pct`, so a multi-day trip with one light day over-reduced the rest. Fixed in two commits: **(1) single-day ergonomics + scope clarity** — `end_date` optional on add (blank → `end==start`; blank *start* still rejected), the list renders a one-day window as `<date> (1 day)` not `X → X`, and the form states the % blankets every covered day; **(2) per-DATE schedule** — a `reduced_volume` window now carries `volume_by_date` (each covered day dials independently; **100% = a normal, unreduced day**). **The plan-gen change is tiny because the per-day union mechanics already existed:** the generator already cuts the plan span at window boundaries and resolves each day against the covering segment's `volume_pct`, so a scheduled window **expands into one-day overrides** in `orchestrator._build_event_window_overlay` (full 1.0 days emit nothing; unmapped dates fall back to the window-wide pct) — segmentation, the per-week capacity factor, the synthesis overlay, and the Rule #15 log all run **unchanged**; a window with **no** schedule stays one override → byte-identical to pre-#889 (regression-tested). **Surface:** `init_db.py` migration (`athlete_event_windows.volume_by_date` TEXT JSON, driver-agnostic like `brought_craft`, NULL = window-wide pct); `orchestrator.py` per-day expansion; `hashing.py` folds `volume_by_date` into `compute_event_windows_hash` (a per-day edit invalidates the overlapping synthesis); `routes/profile.py` + new `templates/profile/event_window_volume_days.html` (strict-CSP-safe per-day editor — one percent select per covered date, reached from a "Per-day levels" link on each multi-day reduced_volume row; Rule #15 log). **`no_training` unchanged** — per-day is reduced_volume-only (`0<pct<=1.0`); a fully-off day stays its own `no_training` window (it also drops the day from the placement pool, which a per-date 0% wouldn't). **VERIFIED:** full suite (merged with latest `main`) **3660 passed / 30 skipped** (+15 new tests: repo load/validate/write, orchestrator per-day expansion + no-schedule regression, hash sensitivity, route GET/POST, render). **DDL auto-applies on deploy** (public-schema `_PG_MIGRATIONS`; no Neon apply owed). **NEXT: back to the #884 thread — slice 4b PR-3** (2C `cluster_gear_toggle_states` un-starve) then slice 4.3.

### Predecessor — Layer 3 #844 3C cross-node conflict detector

**LAYER 3 — #844 3C CROSS-LOCALE / CROSS-SOURCE CONFLICT DETECTOR — SLICES 1+2: NET-NEW DETECTORS (CN-1/CN-2) + SURFACED `coaching_flags` (2026-06-23; branch `claude/eloquent-meitner-86ebqs`; commits `f1b7a86`/`181c5a0`/`b7513c3`; PR [#911](https://github.com/ahorn885/exercise/pull/911) open + auto-merge SQUASH armed; handoff `handoffs/V5_Implementation_Layer3C_ConflictDetection_844_2026_06_23_Closing_Handoff_v1.md`; #844 + #216 closed).** Builds the deferred 3C node off the #216 design-gate. **Design ratified (Andy 2026-06-23, two AskUserQuestion rounds): rules-only (no LLM), scope = net-new conflict detection PLUS surfacing the orphaned upstream `coaching_flags`** — built as two stacked slices on one branch. **3C is purely additive to `evaluate_layer3d_gate`'s §5 step-3 aggregation; the `GateItem`/`Layer3DGate` contract is unchanged.**

**Slice 1 — `map_3c_items(layer2a, layer2c_payloads, layer2d)`** (commit `f1b7a86`): two **warnings**, acknowledge-able, revise → `profile.locales`. **CN-1 `discipline_gated_all_locales`** — an *included* 2A discipline gated off (`toggle_off_for_discipline`/`requires_skill_capability`) at **every** locale (the cross-locale AND no single 2C payload sees). **CN-2 `substitute_gated_all_locales`** — a `high`/`elevated`-risk 2D discipline whose usable (not-`still_at_risk`) `suggested_substitutes` are **all** gated off everywhere; **suppressed** when 2D already emitted `no_substitute_for_high_risk`/`gap_x_high_risk_concurrent`; **mutually exclusive** with the §5.2 `cardio_modality_banned` blocker. Deliberately conservative (every-locale intersection → under-fire not false-fire; zero locales → skipped). `routes/plan_create.py` gains the `"profile.locales" → locales.list_profiles` revise surface.

**Slice 2 — `surface_orphaned_flags(...)`**: the advisory `coaching_flags` from 2A/2B/2C/2D/2E (computed today, silently discarded) now surface as **informational** gate items. **`compute_gate_status` made informational-non-gating** — informational items are display-only, never park a plan (else surfacing would flood every plan to `needs_review`); a plan whose only items are informational stays **green** and proceeds (also relaxes pre-existing 3B `informational` items from gating). **2B threaded in** (`layer2b_payload` added to `evaluate_layer3d_gate`, optional; orchestrator passes `cone.layer2b_payload`; kept out of the §4 etl-coherence check like 2C). All surfaced flags → gate-severity `informational` regardless of source-local severity (2E's own info/low/moderate/high → `evidence['flag_severity']`); **`source='3C'`** (the surfacing node — keeps `GateSource` closed, no `2B`/`2C` enum add), origin in `source_item_id='{origin}:flag:{flag_type}'`; `revise_target` per origin (2A→disciplines, 2B→`h2.*` race editor, 2C→locales, 2D→injuries, 2E→nutrition — all already registered). **Suppression:** a 2C gear/skill flag already escalated to CN-1/CN-2, or a 2D flag whose discipline has a mapped 2D hitl_item, is dropped. **Severity (Andy 2026-06-23 picked "decide at build time → react to a concrete table"):** all 24 builder-emitted flag_types are enumerated + dispositioned in `Layer3D_Spec` **§7.1**; **all-informational at v1**, promotion to gating `warning` = a one-line add to `_FLAG_WARNING` in `gate.py` (top ★ candidates flagged: `unbridgeable_terrain`, `low_calorie_target_relative_to_rmr`; the 2E contraindications are WC but Andy's 2026-06-10 "non-blocking" call argues against). Unknown/stubbed flag_types (e.g. 2E `heat_acclim_gap`, spec'd but §5.8-stubbed) fall through to informational with no 3D change. **Rule #15:** `logger.info` on each CN fire + the surfaced-flag count by origin.

**5 substantive files** (`layer3d/gate.py` / `layer4/orchestrator.py` / `routes/plan_create.py` / `tests/test_layer3d_gate.py` / `specs/Layer3D_Spec.md`). **INTEGRATIONS / #196 — CROSS-SOURCE ACTIVITY DEDUP (PHASE 3) — SLICE 2: THE CLUSTERER (2026-06-23; branch `claude/stoic-albattani-n771ef`; PR [#910](https://github.com/ahorn885/exercise/pull/910) **MERGED** (squash `0054ea9`); `'other'`/unknown is a wildcard that never blocks a start+duration/distance-corroborated merge. **No-fork guarantee:** `pg_advisory_xact_lock(196, user_id)` serializes find-or-create so two near-simultaneous webhooks (Wahoo + its Strava auto-forward) can't both open a cluster (txn-scoped; autocommit off — `database.py`). **NULL `started_at`** → left unclustered (never false-merge; kickoff §6). **Match rule:** start in window AND loose sport AND no metric clearly disagreeing AND ≥1 of duration/distance corroborating — so a bare start coincidence (0 distance + unknown duration) never merges; the indoor repro (distance 0 on both) clusters on duration. **Rule #15:** `[cardio-cluster] … → MATCH/NEW cluster=…` logs inputs + decision + candidate count. **2 substantive files:** `routes/garmin.py` (clusterer + `_coarse_sport`/`_sport_matches`/`_metric_within`/`_fingerprint_match` + constants + the one call site), `tests/test_garmin_bulk_source.py` (`TestCoarseSport` ×4 + `TestClusterActivity` ×8). **No DDL** (Slice 1 substrate already auto-applies) → **no Neon apply owed**. **Tests:** full suite **3491 passed / 30 skipped**; **DESIGN — #593 VOLUME/IN-TRANSIT EVENT WINDOWS + #592 RACE-LOCATION TERRAIN INFERENCE — DESIGN SPECS WRITTEN (2026-06-21; branch `claude/issues-593-592-6llvfq`; PR opened + auto-merge armed on Andy's "open the pr and merge it").** Design-first session (no build), both specs in `designs/`. **#593 `Event_Windows_Slice6_VolumeWindows_Spec_v1.md`:** the deferred F9 `reduced_volume` flag → two new `athlete_event_windows.override_type` values, `reduced_volume` + `no_training`, modeled as their own types that **union** with the feasibility overrides (Slice-1 overlap path). **Resolution model settled (Andy 2026-06-21, after two corrections):** NOT the reallocate→reformat→drop cascade my first draft proposed (Andy: that "introduces multiple new points of failure with the LLM looking for days or time slots it can't find") — instead a **deterministic capacity reduction** feeding the existing grid. Per windowed week compute a capacity factor (`no_training` day = 0 + removed from the placement pool; `reduced_volume` day = the window's athlete-set `volume_pct`), scale the week's target hours by it, and call `session_grid._allocate_discipline` unchanged → fewer/shorter sessions fall out of the existing hours→count math. **Session count ≤ available days by construction → no off-limit slot for the LLM to fail to find** (the whole point). No trim-to-fit, no priority list, no volume conservation (a travel week is honestly lighter). The grid's existing phase logic protects key structure. **#592 `Race_Location_Terrain_Inference_Spec_v1.md` (Andy approved as-spec'd):** a new LLM terrain inference (Trigger #1 — I/O contract spec'd, prompt body owed at build) that pre-fills the today-manual-only `_race_terrain_editor.html` as a reviewable suggestion (never auto-committed); weather **reuses** the existing `weather_client.get_expected_conditions` normals (no new weather inference); **no plan-gen change** — 592 just populates `race_terrain`, which then flows the existing `race_terrain → Layer 2B → orchestrator` path. Carve is clean (a middle step between the race-logging UI and existing 2B consumption); crowd-sourced shared race-profile convergence noted as the future tie-in, not v1. **Andy decisions 2026-06-21 (folded into both specs): #593 `reduced_volume` = a per-window slider (`volume_pct` column, athlete-set, default ~0.5) — NOT a fixed constant; #592 storage = persisted `race_terrain_suggested` column; #592 terrain breakdown = per-discipline (scoped per `discipline_id`, pct sums ~100 within each discipline).** **Remaining sign-off (at build only): Trigger #1 wording — #593 overlay clause + #592 inference prompt body; #592 trigger timing (sync-at-save vs lazy-at-render).** **NEXT:** build each spec (one small slice apiece) when scheduled.

### Predecessor — #424 v2 per-athlete load-progression grid

**LAYER 4 — #424 v2 PER-ATHLETE LOAD-PROGRESSION GRID (3A coupling: trajectory / data-density / ACWR) — BUILT (2026-06-20; branch `claude/issue-424-c9hum9`; PR pending Andy's go [PR-gated]).** Committed v2 follow-up to the #316 per-week volume-periodization grid (PR #422), which was **athlete-agnostic** (one fixed ramp/deload shape scaled only by the 2A bands). **Andy design-picks (AskUserQuestion ×3): (1) scope = ramp steepness AND deeper deload when fatigued; (2) accept the proposed v1-default magnitudes; (3) `recent_trajectory.medium_term.direction` drives the ramp shape.** New `periodization.ramp_modulation_for(layer3a_payload) → RampModulation(ramp_step_factor, deload_multiplier)` maps three 3A signals to the loading curve: **trajectory** (`building`→×1.15 steeper / `fatigued`·`overreached`·`detrained`→×0.85 gentler), **data_density** (`recent_workouts_count` <5→×0.80, <12→×0.90 — sparse → conservative, Spec §8.2 intent), **ACWR** (zone `non_functional_overreach`→×0.70 / `functional_overreach`→×0.85 cap; keyed on the 3A zone so the no-chronic-base sentinel caps correctly; never *accelerates* on ACWR alone), product clamped to [0.5,1.5]. The factor scales the **ramp STEP (slope)**, not absolute levels, so the Base/Build/Peak phase-mean renormalization keeps the **volume-neutral invariant for free** (a capped ramp just flattens the phase, never changes the total — that stays the 2A allocation's job). Fatigue (`fatigued`/`overreached`/`detrained` OR `non_functional_overreach`) ALSO **deepens the deload** (`_M_DELOAD` 0.55 −0.075/signal, floor 0.40 = 60% cut, bottom of the cited 30–60% band); renormalization keeps it volume-neutral → a sharper recovery dip, not a smaller phase. **Single chokepoint:** both consumers (validator band `validator.phase_week_volume_bands_hours`; prompt target `session_grid.build_session_grid` ← `per_phase._format_session_grid` ← `render_user_prompt`) route through `phase_week_multipliers_for_phase`, so threading `layer3a_payload` (already on `ctx.layer3a_payload` validator-side + a `render_user_prompt` param) into that one path keeps band + prompt automatically consistent. **Default `None` → `NEUTRAL_MODULATION` → the v1 athlete-agnostic curve** (graceful degradation; every existing test + payload-less entry point unchanged). Magnitudes are v1 defaults (`_K_*`/`_DELOAD_DEEPEN_STEP`), tune post-launch per Spec §8.3. **Rule #15:** `periodization.log_ramp_modulation` emits the per-athlete decision once per phase render (the pure `ramp_modulation_for` runs per memoized phase-week, so the log lives at the prompt-build path, not the hot fn). **No schema/contract/cache-revision change** (deterministic grid math; prompt *wording* unchanged → no `LAYER4_PROMPT_REVISION` bump). Files: `layer4/periodization.py` (+modulation), `layer4/validator.py`, `layer4/session_grid.py`, `layer4/per_phase.py` (threading) + `tests/test_layer4_periodization.py` (+10 cases: per-signal mapping, clamp, volume-neutrality preserved under modulation, threading, defensive log). **Full suite 3050 passed / 30 skipped.** **LIVE-VERIFY owed (Andy-action — container can't run plan-gen):** regen a plan for a `building` vs a `fatigued`/high-ACWR athlete → `/admin/logs` shows the `ramp_modulation:` line + the loading weeks ramp steeper/flatter and the deload dips deeper respectively (green suite covers the math, not the live curve). **NEXT:** await Andy's "open the PR".

the LLM keeps only exercise selection. **`session_grid.py`:** `compute_recovery_placement(...)` (the single source of truth for both render + validator — `light`=unconstrained, `moderate`=anchor day-after-long & off the long day, `extreme`=off long-day + pre-key day; clamp to feasible days) + `classify_recovery_load_band` (capacity vs phase total band `[low,high]`; Peak/deload→extreme) + shared `derive_enabled_days`/`derive_long_session_dow`. **`per_phase.py`:** `_format_recovery_programming` renders explicit assigned dates ("place a recovery session on <dates> — ASSIGNED; do not add/drop/move") instead of a count + **suppress-on-empty** (no block when the pool resolves empty → kills the unfillable-payload retry); `_format_daily_windows_schedule` single-sources the long day via `derive_long_session_dow` so it can't drift from placement. **`validator.py`:** new `_rule_recovery_placement_match` (D6 blocker — week's `kind=='recovery'` dates must equal `compute_recovery_placement(...)`; lazy-imports to dodge the cycle; guarded on grid-in-context) + `daily_windows_from_layer1` helper. **`hashing.py`:** `LAYER4_PROMPT_REVISION "8"→"9"`. **ANDY-RATIFIED DEVIATION (chat 2026-06-18):** discovered `daily_availability_windows` was **never threaded into the prod `ValidatorContext`** (only tests) — so `daily_window_fit` (blocker), `schedule_violation`, AND the new D6 rule were all **dormant in prod**. Andy chose to thread it in (`plan_create.py` + `per_phase.py` ctx) → D6 is now prod-enforced BUT this **activates `daily_window_fit` as a prod blocker for the first time** (5th substantive file). **Live watch-out:** both `daily_window_fit` + `recovery_placement_match` are now live blockers → an over-full assigned recovery day (2 training + 18 min > window) is a genuine infeasibility that will block + churn — diagnosable (both rule_names co-occur in the per-block failed-rules log); low risk for Andy's generous windows; if it bites live it's a policy call (which rule yields). ### Predecessor — Standing exercises-FK validator added to validate_layer0 (#648)

**LAYER 0 — STANDING EXERCISES-FK VALIDATOR added to `validate_layer0` (#648 CLOSED completed; 2026-06-16; PRs [#651](https://github.com/ahorn885/exercise/pull/651) validator+`0010` + [#653](https://github.com/ahorn885/exercise/pull/653) apply-ledger, both MERGED; branch `claude/layer0-exercises-fk-validator-648`; new validator `etl/layer0/validation/exercises_fk_check.py`; handoff `handoffs/V5_Implementation_Layer0_ExercisesFKValidator_648_2026_06_16_Closing_Handoff_v1.md`).** Continued the "Locations & Gear" arc after #644 closed (Andy chose #648 via `AskUserQuestion`). **The gap (found during #644):** `validate_layer0` FK-checks only the **disciplines** family (`fk_checks.py` — `discipline_substitutes`, `discipline_training_gaps`); **nothing validated the exercises graph.** A kept exercise pointing at a superseded/missing `progression_exercise_id` / `regression_exercise_id` / `physical_proxies[].exercise_id` — or an active `sport_exercise_map.exercise_id` mapping a retired exercise — would **not** fail the gate. The 2C/2D readers filter `superseded_at IS NULL` on the *direct* exercises join so a stale `sport_exercise_map` row goes inert on its own, but a dangling proxy/progression ref on an **active** row would surface (Tier-3 proxy / progression display) uncaught. likewise every active `sport_exercise_map.exercise_id`. **Fix-not-waive** (mirrors the `0006` `primary_movement_check` precedent); wired into the `CHECKS` registry in `validate_layer0.py` (11 entries now) so it runs automatically in the **CI `layer0-gate`** AND the **nightly `layer0-validate-live`** vs prod — **no workflow change.** **The validator immediately earned its keep:** its first gate run **caught 11 pre-existing dangling refs** the #644 verification never saw (that check only scanned refs *into the cull set*). **10 active exercises reference 5 exercise_ids that were NEVER created** (phantom progression/regression/proxy targets named during curation but never added — names don't resolve to any real exercise either): **EX059** "Neck Isometric Hold" (proxy of EX057/058/069/140/158), **EX193** "Shooting Breath Control & Stance" (proxy of EX139/194 + regr of EX194), **EX141** "Wetsuit Swimming Technique" (regr of EX176), **EX147** "Loose Surface Threshold Braking" (regr of EX184), **EX204** "On-Water Boat Balance Drill" (prog of EX200). **Decision (Andy via `AskUserQuestion`):** **STRIP all 11** (over authoring the missing exercises — Trigger #2 padding; most names are non-exercise cues). **Migration `etl/migrations/layer0/0010_strip_dangling_exercise_refs.sql`** supersede+reinserts the 10 holders at `0B-v1.6.10`→`0B-v1.6.11` with phantom proxy elements removed + phantom progression/regression id+name cleared (serving-relevant edit, same pattern as `0007`/`0008`/`0009`; atomic DO-block asserts 0 dangling refs remain + 10 reinserted; idempotent; **NO DDL, no `LAYER4_PROMPT_REVISION` bump**). **NOT a Trigger for the validator** (hardening); the strip is Andy-ratified curation. Per-migration DO-blocks become a redundant belt rather than the only guard. **Tests:** `etl/tests/test_validate_layer0.py` +1 (dangling-ref-fails-the-gate) + extractor-id + registry-count(11) assertions — **etl/tests 90 passed.** Container has the psql **client only** (no local PG server) → **CI is the authoritative live-DB gate** (the first run's RED *is* the finding; green expected once `0010` applies in the gate). **APPLY-MODEL BUG found + fixed mid-session (#652, fixed in #653):** the first `layer0-apply` run for `0010` **failed re-applying `0008`** ("expected 4 survivor tokens, found 2") — the workflow re-applied the *whole* `0006`→`0010` chain every run, but each migration's atomic verify-block pins the state right after itself, which a later migration moves on (`0009` superseded EX150/EX153 that `0008` pins; `0010` re-versions EX176 that `0009` pins). CI never caught it (it applies in-order from a clean baseline). **Fix (Andy via `AskUserQuestion`): apply-ledger** — `etl/migrations/layer0/_apply_ledger.sql` creates `layer0._applied_migrations` + seeds `0006`–`0009` as already-applied; `layer0-apply.yml` now applies each `[0-9]*.sql` **exactly once** (skip if in ledger, record after a clean apply); `ci.yml` gate glob narrowed to `[0-9]*.sql` so the bootstrap stays apply-only. So a verify-block only ever runs in-order, right after its own migration. **APPLIED + VERIFIED (2026-06-16):** re-triggered `layer0-apply` ([run 27623585346](https://github.com/ahorn885/exercise/actions/runs/27623585346)) → ledger seeded `0006`–`0009`, skipped all four, applied **only `0010`** (`0010: OK — 11 dangling phantom refs stripped across 10 active exercises; reinserted at 0B-v1.6.11`); read-only `neon-query` ([run 27624398459](https://github.com/ahorn885/exercise/actions/runs/27624398459)) confirms **0 dangling progression/regression/proxy refs, 10 holders at `0B-v1.6.11`, ledger seeded `0006`–`0010`** → **#648 CLOSED completed.** **NEXT (Locations & Gear arc):** [#619](https://github.com/ahorn885/exercise/issues/619) (profile Locations tab + nav IA — pure UI/IA). **STILL OWED (carried):** the post-#572 live **T3 *refresh*** re-verify (Rule #14).

### Predecessor — WS-E2: deterministic strength-saturation cap

**WS-E2 — deterministic strength-saturation cap (dose+2 + reallocate-with-variety) (2026-06-14, PR [#590](https://github.com/ahorn885/exercise/pull/590), squash-merged to `main`, CI-green; closes WS-E2 [#584](https://github.com/ahorn885/exercise/issues/584); branch `claude/next-slice-implementation-37iur2`; handoff `handoffs/V5_Implementation_WSE2_StrengthSaturationCap_2026_06_14_Closing_Handoff_v1.md`; **north-star plan** `plans/Feasibility_Saturation_And_Locale_Retirement_Plan_v1.md` §7).** The §7 WS-E2 saturation backstop — the last code workstream on the locale-retirement/feasibility-saturation plan. Andy picked it via `AskUserQuestion` and ratified the three design forks (Trigger #1/#5 stop-and-ask): **pre-synthesis grid pass**, **proportional-to-load_weight** reallocation, **build-now**. **Shipped:** new pure `session_grid.apply_strength_saturation_cap` runs **after** the §5.1.1 ceiling inside `build_session_grid` (gated on a new `strength_feasibility_tiers` kwarg — bare callers omit it → no cap, mirrors the `available_days`-gated ceiling). Weekly **failover** strength (terrain/craft-infeasible cardio composed as a strength substitution) is capped at `dose + 2` total — a flat **+2 failover headroom every phase** (the prompt-added dose cancels out of the arithmetic). Over-cap excess is **trimmed lowest-priority-first** and **reallocated to feasible (exact/proxy/indoor) disciplines proportional to load_weight** (d'Hondt highest-averages), with a per-discipline absorption ceiling (a discipline can at most **double** in one pass) so volume spreads instead of dumping (Andy's "3 running + 3 cycling → 6 running" failure mode). **Volume-conserving** — sessions move strength→feasible 1:1, so the upstream session ceiling holds; excess no absorber can take **stays as strength** (training time preserved, never dropped — E1/#579 still backstops the same-day collision crash). New `SessionGrid.saturation_note` carries the **Rule #15** decision line, printed by `per_phase` as `strength_saturation_cap:`. **Trigger-#1 prompt edit:** `strength_guidance.py` failover paragraph now states the cap (was "may push total higher… acceptable"). **Scope note (documented limitation):** caps terrain/craft failover only; skill-gated strength (#336, a deliberate safety substitution) is excluded from both trim and absorb (passed in via `skill_gated_ids`). **No new cache surface** (pure function of already-keyed inputs: feasibility via #556, skill-gated via #336). **NO DDL.** Tests: new `tests/test_layer4_session_grid_saturation.py` (11 cases). **Full suite green (2391 passed, 30 skipped).** **3 substantive files** (`session_grid.py`, `per_phase.py`, `strength_guidance.py`) + 1 new test — within the 5-file ceiling. **NEXT:** plan §2 remaining — WS-V vocabulary arc (durable), WS-H away-craft (needs DDL/design-first); off-plan #542 nutrition macros / #543 health-condition dropdown (Trigger #2) + compliance epics. **STILL OWED (carried):** the post-#572 live **T3 *refresh*** re-verify (paired: diag token + Andy pasting logs, Rule #14). **Minor watch:** a capped-saturated week (dose+2 strength) trips the advisory `_rule_strength_frequency_band` warning (±1 band) by design — non-blocking; bump to ±2 if the noise bothers.

**T3 plan-refresh truncation fix — size synthesis output budget to the session ceiling (2026-06-13, PR [#572](https://github.com/ahorn885/exercise/pull/572))** (branch `claude/adoring-mccarthy-su0igw`, squash-merged to `main`; handoff `handoffs/V5_Implementation_T3RefreshOutputBudgetTruncationFix_2026_06_13_Closing_Handoff_v1.md`). **Ran the live T3 re-verify owed by #569 — #569's `plan_start_date` fix is confirmed live (pv=67 cleared `_validate_inputs`), and the watch caught a *second* shipping bug.** pv=67 (`created_via=plan_refresh_t3`) reached real synthesis but failed `schema_violation … stop_reason=max_tokens, last_attempt_output_tokens=10000/ceiling=10000`: the refresh tiers carried flat output budgets that never absorbed the create path's per-session sizing, so a T3 cross-phase block (up to 56 sessions in one `record_refresh_sessions` call) truncated on a flat 10000 ceiling (~178 tok/session vs the create path's 1400). Because the truncation is a *retryable* `schema_violation`, pv=67 stayed `generating` and the every-minute cron deterministically re-drove it (advance lock 04:12→04:24) — never `ready`. **Fix (Andy's call — reuse the create-path balancing, not decomposition):** new `per_phase.block_output_budget(max_sessions, floor)` = `sessions × 1400 + 2000`, clamped to `_MODEL_MAX_OUTPUT_TOKENS=64000` (the `claude-sonnet-4-6` per-request output ceiling); the refresh driver `llm_layer4_plan_refresh` sizes `effective_max_tokens` to each tier's session ceiling via `_TIER_MAX_SESSIONS` (T1 7,600 / T2 21,600 / **T3 80,400→64,000 clamped**); T3 `DEFAULT_EXTENDED_THINKING_BUDGET` 6500→0 (under thinking the request is `max_tokens + thinking`, so a 64K output budget needs thinking off to stay under the model ceiling — mirrors `per_phase`). The create per-phase block-mode now calls the same helper — **behavior-preserving** (its per-week blocks are ≤21,600, clamp is a no-op). +4 tests; full suite **2366 passed / 30 skipped**; CI green. **Code-only, NO DDL.** **OWED — live T3 re-verify (Andy's hands, post-#572):** re-run a T3 refresh on prod → confirm the new pv reaches `ready` with a phase-correct `total_sessions` (diag token); #572 covers realistic ~20–35-session 4-week windows (≈28–49k, under 64K). **Two optional/contingent follow-ups filed** ([#574](https://github.com/ahorn885/exercise/issues/574) decompose T3 per-week — the create machinery NOT ported, refresh is single-call; [#575](https://github.com/ahorn885/exercise/issues/575) per-pass give-up backstop so a retryable failure stops cron re-driving — adjacent to #539), both `status:deferred`/`priority:low`, build only if their trigger fires. **NEXT:** unchanged — the #541/#542/#543 plan-quality batch, then the compliance build-out (epics #353/#355/#356/#359).

### Predecessor — #334 fixed: event-mode plans reach race day with a 2-week terminal Taper

**Closed the #334 go-live blocker: event-mode plans were stopping ~1 week short of race day and dropping the Taper.** Two compounding bugs: (1) 3B `_time_to_event_weeks` floored (`days // 7`) → a 48-day gap resolved to 6 weeks not 7, dropping the final partial week; (2) `_allocate_weeks_standard`'s `int()` truncation floored a sub-1-week Taper to 0 → it was dropped → `scope_end_date` landed on Peak's end (which *also* silently kills the Decision-4 race-week brief + Taper `coaching_flags`, both of which only attach to an existing Taper). **Fix (spec-first, two amendments then code):** 3B horizon → race-day-inclusive `ceil((days + 1) / 7)` (the `+1` counts race day so an exact-multiple gap doesn't end a day short; PGE 48-day gap → 7 weeks, ends exactly on race day); Layer 4 event-mode terminal phase floored at **2 weeks** (taper wk + race wk; race week stays the final Taper week, no 5th phase), shortfall reclaimed one week at a time from a non-terminal phase (Base first, else largest) without starving any phase below 1 week. **Safety insulation:** the DNF-recurrence HITL trigger (`weeks < window`) was switched to a local conservative **floor** so the new ceil can't inflate the count past the window boundary and suppress a warning that should fire (a 77-day gap is genuinely inside the 12-week `quad_failure` window). PR split to its own #346 (off main); #345 restored to #333-only + merged. **Known residual → #347:** whole-week structure + no `event_date` clamp can overshoot race day by ≤6 days when race day falls mid-week (exact/no-impact for PGE); trimming needs a session-level clamp. Suite **1851/16**; **no migration**. **Cache note:** the changed `time_to_event_weeks` makes the first post-deploy event-mode gen a cold cone (expected). **Next: re-run the PGE e2e (fresh `pv`)** to confirm the plan spans through 2026-07-17 with a 2-week Taper, then the §14 within-phase coherence read (still owed) → remaining #333 sub-items.

Fix: rebind on hydrate (self-heals the poisoned cache on next read) + force the payload's id at persist (safety net). Suite **1845/16**; no migration. ### Predecessor — plan-gen poller 500 regression fix (PR #312)

`handoffs/V5_Implementation_PlanGen_D77_PollerGeneratingMapping_504GiveUpFix_2026_05_29_Closing_Handoff_v1.md` — 2026-05-29 (**plan-gen poller 500 regression fix — PR #311's two new `'generating'` outcomes were never mapped in the poller route, so every multi-block plan KeyError-500'd to "taking longer than expected"; branch `claude/ecstatic-hamilton-NoWBX`, PR #312**)

**Fixed the regression PR #311 introduced into plan-gen.** PR #311's concurrency guard + per-invocation budget added two `{"status": "generating", ...}` returns to `_advance_plan_generation`, but the poller route `generate_plan` was never taught to handle them — it fell through to `jsonify({"status": "failed", "error": outcome['error']})`, KeyError-ing on the missing `'error'` key → **HTTP 500 on every intermediate poll**. The budget makes `budget_partial_progress` the *normal* path for any plan needing >1 pass, so essentially every real multi-block plan 500'd its way to the client's give-up message ("This is taking longer than expected. Please try again.") even though the cone was healthy and caching blocks. Fix: (1) `generate_plan` now maps `'generating'` → `{"status":"generating"}` (keep-polling); (2) `templates/plan_create/progress.html` replaces the *total*-poll cap (`MAX_ATTEMPTS=20`, far too few now each pass does ~1 week-block) with a *consecutive-transport-failure* cap — a clean response resets it; the server-side 900s wall-clock stall backstop remains the real terminal guard. 2 code/template files + `tests/test_routes_plan_create.py` (+5 `TestGeneratePlanRoute`); 50 passed in that file, 160 combined. **No migration.** **This unblocks the still-owed D-77 convergence re-run** — that gating proof (CARRY_FORWARD owed #1) could never have gone green at the client before, because the poller 500'd on every budget-partial pass. The live code state otherwise matches the predecessor below (D-77 convergence, PR #294/#311, re-run owed).

**Finally read the prod Vercel logs (prior 3 sessions diagnosed code-only) and pinned the actual non-convergence root cause — a SECOND instance of the c4f9160 cache-key non-determinism bug that fix missed.** The two failed `plan_version_id=29` runs 504-looped with `max_tokens=9200` live + `schema_violation` GONE (PR #197 worked) but `accepted=True` never appearing. **Bug A (PR #199, merged):** `Layer2EPayload.computed_at` (`layer2e/builder.py:1156`) was stamped full-microsecond `datetime.now()`; the cone rebuilds every resumable pass, and `computed_at` folds into `layer2e_hash` → `plan_create_key` → EVERY `compute_block_cache_key`, so each pass minted different block keys → every cached block orphaned → re-synthesized from scratch each pass → 504-loop re-burning the full extended-thinking synthesis each minute (the ~$50). Fix: bound `_generation_stalled` + `_count_cached_blocks` to `created_at >= pv.created_at` (per-plan progress only). 2 code + 2 test files across the two PRs + `Layer4_Spec §11.5`. Suite **1796 passed / 16 skipped**. **No migration** (query/sampling-level; existing orphan rows just stop mattering). **⚠ Owed (Andy's hands): merge PR #200 + redeploy, then create ONE fresh plan** — it should now get past the gate (Bug B) and CONVERGE (Bug A). ### Predecessor — D-77 block-mode `max_tokens` truncation fix (full record in `handoffs/`)

`handoffs/V5_Implementation_PlanGen_D77_BlockMaxTokens_SchemaViolationFix_2026_05_27_Closing_Handoff_v1.md` — 2026-05-27 (**D-77 block-mode `max_tokens` truncation fix — the cone/truncation watch-item fired; branch `claude/plan-gen-schema-violation-tpu23`**)

**The cone/truncation fix (PR #195) worked — the re-run no longer 504-looped, but failed with a bounded `schema_violation` ("Plan synthesis failed (schema_violation). Adjust your inputs and try again."), exactly the predecessor's §6/§11.5 watch-item.** The per-block budget guard + empty-tool escalation stopped the loop, but the **forced-tool retry runs with thinking OFF**, so `max_tokens` is the *entire* output budget (no `+ thinking_budget` headroom). The per-phase default `max_tokens=4000` predates the dense `PlanSession` schema (per-session `cardio_blocks` + `strength_exercises` + 240-char notes ≈ 400–600 output tokens), so a full high-frequency week (up to 14 sessions, the PGE 6-discipline norm) truncated mid-`sessions` → incomplete tool call → `schema_violation`. **Fix:** block mode (`week_range` set) now sizes the output budget to the unit's session ceiling — `effective_max_tokens = max(max_tokens, max_sessions_this_unit × _BLOCK_OUTPUT_TOKENS_PER_SESSION(600) + _BLOCK_OUTPUT_TOKENS_OVERHEAD(800))` = **9200** for a 1-week block; never below the caller's value. Higher `max_tokens` is only a ceiling (billed/latency cost tracks emitted tokens; the `_PER_BLOCK_BUDGET_MS=120_000` guard still bounds time) and it also gives the *first* thinking attempt more post-thinking output room. Whole-phase seam-resynth (`week_range=None`, ≤56 sessions) is intentionally NOT scaled — that's the Slice-3 stitcher's path, not a token bump. 1 code file (`layer4/per_phase.py`) + 2 tests (`TestBlockOutputBudget`) + `Layer4_Spec §11.5` in place. Suite **1795 passed / 16 skipped** (+2). **No migration** (`max_tokens` is a sampling param, not in any cache key/schema). **⚠ Owed (Andy's hands): redeploy (merge) + re-run the PGE plan.** **NOTE: diagnosis is code-evidence-based — the prod log was not in hand this session** (Andy pasted only the athlete message). The re-run proof is the per-attempt log line `synthesize_phase: <phase>:w<n> … out=N max_tokens=9200` (`out` should land BELOW the ceiling, not pin it) + the `<phase>:w<n> done — … accepted=True` summary firing. If a `schema_violation` still surfaces, send back that line + the route's `_advance_plan_generation: Layer4 … (schema_violation) … : <detail>` (`detail` carries `stop_reason` + cause) — `stop_reason=max_tokens` near 9200 ⇒ raise further / trim thinking budget; anything else ⇒ a different fix. Coherence (design §14) still UNVERIFIED until a plan reaches `ready`.

### Predecessor — D-77 cone cache-key determinism + synthesizer truncation + per-block budget (full record in `handoffs/`)

`handoffs/V5_Implementation_PlanGen_D77_ConeCacheKeyDeterminism_SynthTruncationFix_2026_05_27_Closing_Handoff_v1.md` — 2026-05-27 (**D-77 non-convergence ROOT CAUSE fixed — cone cache-key determinism + synthesizer truncation + per-block budget; branch `claude/plan-gen-timeout-logs-caH8Q`**)

**The instrumented re-run (`plan_version_id=27`) pinned the stall to TWO independent bugs; fixed both.** (1) **Cone cache keys were non-deterministic across function invocations** — `Layer1Payload.as_of` + `Layer2APayload.rationale_metadata.generated_at` were stamped with full-precision `datetime.utcnow()` and hashed into `layer1_hash`/`layer2a_hash`, which fold into EVERY Layer 4 cache key (3A/3B/`compute_block_cache_key`/refresh/single-session/brief). So 3A + 3B re-ran cold on **every** resumable pass (prod logs: the live-run `Layer3A/3BEvidenceBasisWarning` in 17/17 passes, ~150s/pass) and any synthesized block was orphaned next pass — D-77 monotonic convergence was **structurally impossible**, which is why decomposition never helped (this overturns the predecessor's "warm 3A/3B cone" assumption — it had no per-layer cache instrumentation). Fix: day-anchor both timestamps (matches the 3A `as_of` day-granular cache semantics; neither field is consumed — pure provenance). (2) **The synthesizer starved its own output on the thinking budget** — `attempt 1/3 llm call 142528ms (in=6896 out=9000)` then `tool_args keys=[]`: under thinking the ceiling is `max_tokens(4000)+budget(5000)=9000`, the model spent it all thinking and emitted a contentless tool call → no sessions → never cached. Fix: `invoke_tool_call` treats an empty tool call like a missing block → fires the existing forced-tool retry (thinking off → full output budget, can't decline). Plus a structural **per-block budget** (`_PER_BLOCK_BUDGET_MS=120_000`) in `synthesize_phase`: once a block spends its LLM-time budget it won't start another attempt — accepts best-effort (caches → progress) or fails terminally fast (`synthesis_budget_exhausted`), never 504-loops. 4 code files (`layer1/builder.py`, `layer2a/builder.py`, `llm_invocation.py`, `layer4/per_phase.py`) + 13 tests (escalation ×10, hash-determinism ×2, budget-guard ×1) + `Layer4_Spec §11.5` updated in place. Suite **1793 passed / 16 skipped** (+13). **No migration.** **⚠ Owed (Andy's hands): redeploy (merge), then re-run the PGE plan** — expect it to CONVERGE now (3A/3B cache after pass 1 → blocks cache → `ready`). Watch the Vercel log: `synthesize_phase: <phase>:w<n> done — …` should fire (it never has), and the cone should NOT re-run 3A/3B every pass. If the forced-tool retry still truncates a dense ~14-session week against `max_tokens=4000`, the follow-on is bumping block-mode `max_tokens` (the budget guard keeps it failing fast, not looping, meanwhile).

### Predecessor — D-77 per-block budget instrumentation (full record in `handoffs/`)

`handoffs/V5_Implementation_PlanGen_D77_PerBlockBudget_Instrumentation_2026_05_27_Closing_Handoff_v1.md` — 2026-05-27 (**D-77 per-block synthesis-budget finding + diagnostic instrumentation; branch `claude/plan-generation-timeout-8s1Hn`**)

**Found why the re-run STILL stalled, then shipped logging-only instrumentation (Andy's gate: "add logging first").** Andy re-ran the coherence walk on the deployed wall-clock-backstop fix (#189, now under prod #190) and got the same "Plan generation stalled." The prod runtime log for `plan_version_id=25` shows: 3A/3B were warm cache hits (cone NOT the bottleneck), week-1 block synthesis was reached immediately, then **every** generate pass (poller + cron) 504'd with an `api.anthropic.com` call in flight, and the wall-clock backstop tripped at ~960s with **zero blocks cached**. **Root cause:** a single week-block's `synthesize_phase` retry loop (up to `capped_retries+1`=3 extended-thinking calls, ×a forced-tool fallback) is **in-memory / not resumable across function invocations**, and the block caches only after the loop returns — so a block that needs retries exceeds the immovable 300s cap, 504-kills mid-loop, caches nothing, and restarts from attempt 1 next pass: an infinite loop, the SAME failure as the original `plan_version_id=23` incident. D-77 Slice 1 shrank the *cache unit* (phase→week) but never bounded a single block's *synthesis cost*. The backstop is healthy; the unit still doesn't fit. At an `AskUserQuestion` gate Andy chose **"add logging first"** over committing to a fix — so this session is **instrumentation only, no behavior change**: `layer4/per_phase.py` now logs per-attempt LLM latency + the previously-silent per-block validator-rejection rule set (+ parse / no-`sessions` detail + a per-block summary) under a greppable `<phase>:w<week>` tag. `Layer4_Spec §11.5` records the open limitation. Suite **1780 passed / 16 skipped** (unchanged — pure `print`). **No migration. ⚠ Owed (Andy's hands): redeploy (merge), re-run the PGE plan (it will likely stall again — that's expected; the goal is the logs), then send back the `synthesize_phase:` log lines** so next session reads *why* blocks retry and picks the bounding fix (candidates: per-block wall-clock budget → best-effort; lower retry/thinking budget; finer decomposition — all Trigger #5).

### Predecessor — D-77 Slice 2 backstop fix (full record in `handoffs/`)

`handoffs/V5_Implementation_PlanGen_D77_Slice2_BackstopWallClockFix_2026_05_27_Closing_Handoff_v1.md` — 2026-05-27 (**D-77 Slice 2 backstop fix — wall-clock stall gate; branch `claude/gallant-gates-DWmb6`**)

**Fixed the Slice 2 progress backstop, which was false-failing plans ~46s in.** The first real-LLM coherence walk (`plan_version_id=24`) hit "Plan generation stalled," but the Vercel log showed a single in-flight Anthropic call and **no `schema_violation`** — so the Slice 2 backstop was strangling the run, NOT the decomposition. The stall trip was a per-CALL counter (`_STALL_PASS_LIMIT=2`), and both the every-minute cron and the progress poller call `_advance_plan_generation` on the same `generating` row → poller-start ticked it to 1, the cron 43s later to 2, killing the plan before its first ~300s week-block could cache. Fix: a **wall-clock gate** (`_generation_stalled`, `_STALL_WALLCLOCK_S=900`) — trip only when no block has cached for ~3 function budgets, measured on the DB clock (`NOW()` vs. the newest block's `created_at`, else generation start); robust to a 504-killed pass and to concurrent cron/poller calls. Migration-free (existing `created_at`); `generation_stall_passes` retained-but-unused. `Layer4_Spec §11.5` + the `init_db.py` schema comment amended in place. Suite **1780 passed / 16 skipped** (+3). **⚠ Decomposition convergence is still UNVERIFIED** — the backstop never let the first block finish. **Next:** Andy redeploys (merge) + re-runs the coherence walk, which now actually exercises per-week synthesis (does it reach `ready`? do the independently-generated weeks blend within a phase? — design §14).

### Earlier predecessor (full record in `handoffs/`)

`handoffs/V5_Implementation_PlanCreate_Layer3B_SectionH2_GoalContextScalars_2026_05_26_Closing_Handoff_v1.md` — 2026-05-26 (**§H.2 deployed-shape gap — scalar goal-context capture (Slice 1 of 2); branch `claude/v5-implementation-blockers-PV5LH`; PR #184**)

**Closed the high-value half of the Layer 3B §H.2 deployed-shape gap — the athlete can now state their actual race goal, and Layer 3B reads it.** 3B's event-mode goal-viability + HITL machinery was designed to read the athlete's goal fields, but the deployed `race_events` row never stored three of them — the cached wrapper hardcoded `goal_outcome="Finish"`, so every athlete was treated as a finisher regardless of ambition (viability skewed optimistic; the `3B.first_time_competitive_goal` HITL flag could never fire).
